# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# OpenJDK G1 GC Garbage Collection Cycle Chain

## Your Task

Trace the G1 garbage collector's concurrent marking and mixed collection cycle in openjdk/jdk. Find C++ source files implementing: the G1ConcurrentMark start trigger, the SATB marking queue processing, the remembered set scanning, and the mixed collection region selection.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo domain.

## Available Resources

- `sg-evals/jdk--742e735d` (openjdk/jdk)

## Summary of Findings

The answer includes:

### **17 Key C++ Source Files** implementing:
- **G1ConcurrentMark** (hpp/cpp) - Main concurrent marking class managing the cycle
- **G1ConcurrentMarkThread** (hpp/cpp) - Thread controlling marking phases
- **G1Policy** (hpp/cpp) - Triggers marking cycle based on heap occupancy
- **G1RemSet** (hpp/cpp) - Remembers set scanning during collection
- **G1CollectionSet** (hpp/cpp) - Selects old regions for mixed collection
- **SATBMarkQueue** (hpp/cpp) - Snapshot-At-The-Beginning barrier implementation
- **G1BarrierSet** (hpp/cpp) - Write barrier integration
- And supporting infrastructure files

### **Key Components in the Execution Chain**:

1. **Cycle Trigger**: `G1Policy::initiate_conc_mark()` - Decides when to start based on heap occupancy
2. **Cycle Start**: `G1ConcurrentMark::concurrent_cycle_start()` - Initializes GC timing
3. **SATB Activation**: `SATBMarkQueueSet::set_active_all_threads()` - Enables write barrier
4. **Root Region Scan**: `G1ConcurrentMark::scan_root_regions()` - Initial scanning phase
5. **Main Marking**: `G1ConcurrentMark::mark_from_roots()` - Concurrent marking with parallel tasks
6. **Queue Drainage**: `G1CMTask::drain_satb_buffers()` - Processes references from SATB barrier
7. **RemSet Scanning**: `G1RemSet::scan_heap_roots()` - Scans remembered sets
8. **Region Selection**: `G1CollectionSet::select_candidates_from_marking()` - Chooses old regions for mixed GC

This is actually safe, since the entering the sync\n948:  * barrier is one of the last things do_marking_step() does, and it\n949:  * doesn't manipulate any data structures afterwards.\n950:  */\n951: ",
    "url": "https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/jdk--742e735d@b394eab7f7a9ef928dbbcac1e27e0a0b1577894a/-/blob/src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1ConcurrentMark.cpp%3FL900-950"
